Because that heart was strong, heaven has endured until now, knowing that there will be a day when it will meet that substantial form.

Jesus had the gift of resurrection after the cross, but He could not boast of that day. He set the hopeful day of "I will come again" and left. For 2,000 years, He has been fighting while longing for that day of return. Just as heaven has done so, we on earth must also follow that path. Furthermore, we must become a group that knows there is a history of heaven's effort to establish that original self, and we must have a heart that can be concerned about heaven's face and dignity.

We must be able to sing about the historical hopeful day. In other words, we must think about what kind of self I will be when I meet the Lord of resurrection coming in glory, and we must have a firm standard regarding that self, making a resolution and vow to go until the day we find it, no matter what happens. If we fail to do this, we cannot deny that our faith life until today has been a life that rather violates me.

Through the 2,000 years of history after Jesus, heaven has endured while looking forward to the hopeful day of return. When we think about the footprints of the historical path, it is only natural that I serve my family and seek to encourage my family. In seeking that day to meet the bridegroom, these are adornments and decorations that a bride must have, and we must be able to appreciate and rejoice in them, shedding tears before the Father. 

The heavenly world is vast and infinite. When we go out with the heart that one existence in that world is an infinite existence, Jesus will find us and welcome us as we come with hope. That time will be your spiritual experience time, a time to meet Jesus in the spiritual realm. Therefore, I hope that the heart to meet Him will deeply resonate within you. Those without that heart will not be able to find the second self to stand before the Father, and they will ultimately reach the conclusion that they cannot stand before the Father.

The reason patience is needed in faith is that one must become one who knows how to endure. God has also endured. From the day sin was committed in Eden until today, the historical process has been a process of endurance, and no one can deny that. Even when tracing God's footsteps towards nations, we know that He has walked a path of tears and blood while enduring. 

Moreover, look at the history of Christianity. Even when enemies mocked His beloved only son and made Him a sacrifice of death, God has endured. 

The chosen nation of Israel has never been free from oppression throughout its long history, and there has never been a time when it was not oppressed. So why has the God of that nation, the God of that people, endured until now? It is because humanity, which fell due to inability to endure, is in a fate where God cannot help but endure until the day of victory is established by those who can endure. 

Until we find the self that can endure, God's heart cannot be resolved. In other words, we must resolve God's heart by enduring, we must resolve the nation by enduring, and we must resolve the universe by enduring, hoping for a day of happiness. Until we meet individuals, families, nations, and countries that remain even in the paths of struggle, persecution, and death, we cannot conclude the history of endurance and cannot exercise judgment.

You must understand that for 6,000 years, God has endured with a heart filled with resentment, and even though He has the authority to judge, He has not judged but has endured. Therefore, we must start with endurance and conclude with endurance. 

In Christianity, there is the noun of judgment, but what is that judgment? It is the time when heaven can conclude the history of endurance. Heaven has endured while longing for that time. That is something God Himself cannot resolve; it can only be resolved through people. We must become a Christianity that can step forward with the authority of judgment and judge the enemies. And we must have the support of God's endurance over the 6,000 years. 

We must feel the heart of the Father who has endured throughout history, and we must be those who can step forward with the determination to say, "Father! Please release the heart that has endured and let me fulfill the mission of restoration through me." 

There must be those who can step forward with such a resolve. For 6,000 years, heaven has established its will and has gone through an indescribably immense history of struggle with the ancestors. You must appear with a heart that combines all of your hearts with the heart of God who has endured, and you must have a heart of abundance that can endure. Otherwise, God's...
You cannot surpass the threshold of the heart you have been enduring, nor can you establish the criteria for resolution that arises from it, and thus you cannot hasten the judgment. Heaven has warned us that there will be a seven-year great tribulation at the end. And the words spoken for the saints say that in the end, even the chosen ones will be deceived. You all know well that it is said that those who endure until the end in this tribulation will be saved.

The destination of endurance
So where is the destination of that endurance? Where is the endpoint of patience? Have you all wandered and searched for that endpoint? Was it in the family of Adam? No, it was not there. Was it in the family of Noah? No, it was not there either. Was it in the prophets of old? No, it was not there either. Today, even within my own being, the history of endurance remains, and in this society, the history of endurance remains, and when I think that the history of endurance will remain for my descendants, I must appear before the Father as one qualified as a prince of endurance. There must be those on this earth who at least have the thought of going before Heaven with the heart to comfort the Father who has endured for six thousand years.

You may have endurance, but you will realize that this endurance is far from the historical endpoint of endurance. Today, I hear people connected to our church say, "I can't go because it's difficult." They say the Unification Church is good, but they can't go because it's hard. The ones who can say that are probably the happy ones. They may seem happy when viewed from the ground, but from Heaven's perspective, they are pitiful. Indeed, it is truly difficult to go. The path is a path of tears. It is a path of seeing and crying, feeling and crying, fighting and crying. I thought the time for tears would end here, but it is not. I realize that the tears must continue, and that Heaven has a heart that longs for more tears of endurance. When I understand that Heaven is waiting for us, who appear in such pitiful forms, I have no face to show before Heaven for the fact that I endured. The Teacher has come this far since liberation, but I have not yet considered the limits of my endurance. I do not wish for it to end either. From the moment I wish for it to end, I will begin to examine myself, and from that moment, I will feel fear, which you must experience in your faith life.

Have you ever deeply considered that the enduring Father, who is my Father, is the one with whom I will live forever, and that the enduring one is the bridegroom I will serve? It is likely that you have not. Let us say there is one who rejoices and enjoys glory before Heaven. The one who appears before Heaven in the form of endurance is more precious than those who are happy in the historical process of endurance in today’s chaotic history.

You must be those who understand this attitude of a believer. Those who do not know how to overcome this chaotic era with such a heart will become traitors to Heaven. 

Do you have suffering due to material things? You must endure this. Do you have suffering due to knowledge? You must endure this too. Do you have psychological suffering regarding your own self? You must endure this as well. To avoid becoming one who betrays the six-thousand-year history of endurance, you must endure, endure, and endure again. What you thought was lost has become Heaven's history, and what you thought was collapsing has emerged as Heaven's history.

You are well aware of the Six Martyred Scholars. It was because of the Six Martyred Scholars, including Seong Sam-mun. You must understand that the path of endurance, the path of death, and any place of suffering, including the harsh swords and spears, have supported our national spirit.

Then who will inherit Heaven's traditional, heavenly spirit today? It is those who highly regard the altar of endurance. You must understand that those who uphold the altar of endurance and long for Heaven are the ones. How will the world overcome the peaks of suffering it must face? How will Heaven overcome this peak? If, after building the fortress of suffering and the fortress of death, welfare does not appear, then God's endurance cannot see an end on any given day.

Where to find true leaders
Today, we call ourselves believers. We claim to seek the ideals of Heaven. We sing of tomorrow's life, seek tomorrow's hope, and base ourselves on tomorrow's nation, tomorrow's people, tomorrow's ethnicity, tomorrow's family, and tomorrow's self. This is the path of faith, but that tomorrow's self is still far away. That self does not exist in today. If you search for it here, you will all be disheartened. It does not exist around you either. You must first walk the path of suffering that you should walk and raise the standard of the earnest heart you should long for. As long as there is a history of humanity to establish, you must understand that until this is resolved, that day will not come.

Our steps are those of the heavenly soldiers who have prepared to march for the sake of the ideals of hope, and those steps must go forward without knowing anything but the front. You must not turn back when you hear a voice from behind. That is the voice of the enemy. You must not get close to those who are friendly beside you. You must know that they are enemies who seek your life. There are no true friends in the environment you live in. 

There are no true leaders in your journey. You will only find true heavenly leaders when you seek true truth and true leaders with a sincere heart. If you have a false heart, no matter how true they are, they will become false. In the historical process, even if you have a true connection to life, there have been twists and turns that had to appear as false connections to life. You must seek truth from your heart. You must seek the teacher of truth from your heart, seek the household of truth from your heart, seek the hometown of truth from your heart, and seek the nation of truth from your heart. And you must think of the ideals of hope as the focal point. Furthermore, you should fight against the environmental darkness centered around that and boast of that connection, longing for the realization of hope. When you can proudly show this true self and break through the surrounding environment, only then will Heaven's work be accomplished.

Therefore, when you take the final step at the decisive line of ultimate victory and break that line, a new hope will appear to you. You will greet a new day. You will possess a new ideal as your own. To make that new ideal your own, you must understand that there are heavenly conditions that require you to walk such a path. Therefore, we, who are facing such a historical destiny, must have a firm resolution.

Now, from this perspective, reflect on yourselves. Do I truly have the attitude of a believer? Was my faith to establish a heart of hope? Was I the one who longed for that? If you think that everything will be fine with your old faith and that you can solve everything, you will not be able to walk that path. 

Because we must possess the correct attitude of faith, even if the power of death strikes us, we must have enough left over to overcome that power of death. There must be remaining traces. My zeal must remain, my loyalty must remain, my efforts must remain, my endurance must remain, and everything belonging to me must have a field that remains. This must be understood as the first standard of Heaven's inheritance.

To go through today's complicated forms, you must seek that hope. You must carry the historical connections, the temporal connections, and the future connections in your heart, longing for this hope of self. 4) The path of faith that must be carefully observed
Matthew 11:1-30
<Prayer (I)> As unworthy beings, we have come out again to bow our hearts and bodies before the holy image of the Father, longing for it, so please regard us with the grace of compassion. Father, who does not abandon us and guides us with new love without ceasing! The place where we receive the love of the Father is a place that all created beings admire, a place that countless people in the past have admired, and a place that present and future humans must admire. Please allow us to appear as earnest sons and daughters who can call upon the Father with such a heart and hold onto the Father. 

Those who seek the Father with earnest hearts and worry about the Father's circumstances know that the Father will not abandon them, so please allow our hearts to run toward the Father's heart, and allow our bodies to run to be embraced in the Father's arms. May the movement to break away from the sorrowful history of sin fill our hearts and bodies at this time, and may our hearts and bodies be stirred, we earnestly hope and desire.

We are weak beings who cannot take confident steps to seek Heaven, so we hope that the Father will remain as the Lord of faith. The earth is rough, and the difficult path of tribulation remains, and although we may be weary there, we hope that Heaven will appear strong. 

We did not know that the Father had many times been disheartened after coming to find us, and we did not know that when the Father's hopes for humanity were not fulfilled because of us, the Father had to turn away again. Please let us know that the Father's hopes are greater than our own. May we not forget that the Father wished us to be strong when we are weak and that when He holds onto His will, He seeks strong ones, we earnestly hope and desire.

Now our hearts long for the image of the Father, our bodies want to look upon the form of the Father, our hands want to hold onto the touch of the Father, and we want to hold onto the body of the Father. Knowing that it is the central wish of the Father towards humanity to welcome true sons and daughters who can sing of Your love, may this time be one where at least our hearts can be filled with such feelings. Father, we earnestly hope and desire.

Today, we are stained with sin, we are in darkness, and during this time, our senses and our five senses have been unable to feel the Father's sorrow and sighs, and we have been too busy appealing our own sorrows while forgetting the Father's sorrowful heart.

We, who have nothing to present before the Father, please lead us to have at least a heart that can feel sorrow for ourselves. 

We must be able to explode with the sad feelings of reproaching the past wrongs and blaming the present inadequacies from our hearts to call upon the Father, knowing that the Father will hold us, the Father will look upon us, and the Father will embrace us.
Please allow us. With such a heart, we recognize our shortcomings and earnestly wish to manifest a heart that can dedicate everything before our Father. We sincerely hope and desire this, Father. 

Father, please look upon your ashamed children gathered here with compassion. We are aware that there are times when what we thought we knew can be unknown, and we understand that the time has come for us to deny the very act of justifying ourselves with our own words and to be reborn. We know that all historical sorrows cannot be resolved without conditions of indemnity.

Please let us know that a time is coming when we will be placed in the positions of Cain and Abel before your will. When individual hearts and bodies are in conflict, with the body scolding and blaming the heart, and the heart succumbing before the body, we realize that as the time of historical end approaches, the moments that can connect from the individual to the family, church, society, and world are drawing near before our eyes.

We, who know today that our ancestors were led astray by the history of sorrow, are also in a position where we can easily be used as tools to weave a history of sin. However, we recognize that the elements that can be used to build heavenly goodness are exceedingly few. Now, please allow us to know when to close our mouths even if we want to speak, to endure seeing what we do not want to see, and to have the heart that knows to block our ears when we hear words we do not wish to hear.

Even if our hearts that should be directed toward heaven are wandering in confusion, and our bodies are in an environment unable to find a place to rest, we believe that you will not abandon us but will lead us into your embrace with the hand of grace. Therefore, we earnestly hope and desire that you will look upon us with compassion and raise in us a heart that can kneel and appeal before you, Father.

We fear becoming traitors to heaven who stir up eternal sorrow by lacking such a heart, so please make us those who hold onto ourselves and weep. Rather than lamenting over our brothers, let us lament over our own hearts, and if we do not feel the desire to help our neighbors who may be in the same sorrowful position as us, we know we will not be able to overcome the final hill we must cross at the end. Therefore, Father, at this time, please encourage the hearts of our beloved family members.

Let us know what the purpose of your providence is and what your hope is until now, and let us analyze, establish, and guard the content we must decide before you in our hearts. We earnestly hope and desire this.

Father, on this holy day, please bless countless humanity and bless the many sons and daughters of yours gathered here.

There are countless sons and daughters calling you Father, yet there are very few true sons and daughters who can genuinely call you Father, who can say, "My sons and daughters." Who can stop this sadness? Who can comfort your sorrow? We know that there is none on earth.

We know that true sons and daughters who can share your heart and possess this ideology must come to you and embrace you, and that moment must appear at the historical end, at the end of hope.

Father, let your sons and daughters gathered here reflect on whom they have come for, whom they are to support, and whom they are to serve, and let them abandon their frivolous attitudes before the lonely Father and become humble and gentle in appearance. Let us feel the sorrow of your sorrow and be able to comfort you, and may this time be one where we can call upon you, Father.

At this time, there are lonely family members in various places kneeling and praying before you. Father, who knows their circumstances, please do not abandon them but be their sovereign and protector. May all their worries be understood and comforted by you, and may this be a joyful time to sing of your glory.

We, who are lacking, kneel before you to worship, so please sanctify us personally and do not allow any part of Satan from the beginning to the end. We earnestly ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen.

<Prayer (II)> Father, though our path is rough, we know that the day of our wish to meet the people of heaven is not far away, and though our steps may be weary on this path, we realize it is the life path we cannot avoid because it is the path you walked.

<Prayer (III)> We have learned through your words what sorrow leaves behind in the form of nail marks on the heart. Father! Let us understand that the persecution is not persecution but the work of the Father to connect our hearts.

With our hands joined and heads bowed before the Father, may we return the victory of the song of triumph in a place where we can say that the heavenly laws do not contradict the historical path, so that we may indeed become those whom the Father can call His children. 

Let us rejoice together in the Father's joy, and may we raise a heart that cannot help but cause even Satan to blush and not be able to laugh in shame when I rejoice, knowing that the heavens demand the appearance of sons and daughters who can fulfill such a heart. Therefore, I earnestly hope and wish to become Unification Church members who can urge such a self to arise.

What we have desired has been so little. What we have cherished and respected, we thought was the end, but we have come to know that beyond that lies infinite love and infinite grace. 

May the heart that laments that we have been the ones blocking the way before the Father’s grace rise up in this hour among each and every family member. Now, when the heart is stimulated and we are urged to burn with a sense of mission, may we be those who can come joyfully when called and go joyfully when sent. 

If we have been grateful for the voice that calls us, let us also be grateful for the voice that commands us, and may we become heavenly warriors who can charge toward the enemy’s camp, becoming the masters of the heavenly world. We know that there will be those who fall, even in this arena, so please guide us not to become those who retreat in defeat.

While there are moments of happiness in discussing with the Father, there are also moments when these sons and daughters shed tears of blood on the battlefield, appealing to heaven’s grievances and collapsing. 

Let us take responsibility for joy, take responsibility for sorrow, take responsibility for struggle, and take responsibility for injustice, and before the judgment seat of the end times, refuse the historical things. 

Father, raise Your hand and bless us. Father, please bear with the anger You feel when You look at us. Father, please bear with the pain and injustice You feel when You look at me. Father, please take away the labor You have endured when You look at me.

May it be possible. It has been 6,000 years that You have longed for such sons and daughters to appear, and 6,000 years that You have sought them carefully. Father, we are in awe and overwhelmed. We have forgotten the gaze with which You seek, the appearance with which You seek, and the careful footsteps You have taken.

Today, we have heard, and at this moment, we have come to know. We understand that You have told us to seek carefully. We have realized that we have betrayed the hand that sought to hold us, having forgotten the dignity of the Father.

Now let us stand before the Father, live a life connected to the Father, and walk the path we must carefully seek on behalf of the Father. After walking this path, we must teach those who do not know this path how to carefully seek it. We must not become those who shed sad tears and retreat in this place, for we have received such a heavenly command.

We know that the heart of the Father, who sought to love and bless those who betray, remains with anger. Now, as we pray the prayer that Elijah prayed at the end, let us have a heartfelt desire to comfort the one who appears in sorrow, knowing that there is no one to comfort Him.

When the weary footsteps searching for You collapse, and when the careful steps searching for You become exhausted and fall, we long for the moment when You say, "I am here; come to the path I am taking." 

You have known that You could not trust humans to work, and You have been unable to avoid worrying that the work of heaven would be delayed by discussing it with humans.

In this time, we know that many crowds are not needed. This is the time to overcome and move forward, the time to settle and move on, the time to conclude everything and move forward, the time to appear as you are. This path is not one that those who complain can walk, nor can those who make excuses walk it, nor can those who elevate themselves walk it. 

We know that this path is the path of the cross that Jesus walked, the extended path of Golgotha, and thus, while we are bodies that want to make excuses, we do not know how to make excuses. We want to boast of ourselves, but we do not know how to boast, and we know that we must walk this path even while being trampled upon. 

When we think of the heavenly saints who have walked this path over 6,000 years of providential history, we feel wronged. However, when we realize that the Father’s heart is even more wronged, we must repent. 

It is the sorrow of sorrows, a situation that must be regretted beyond words. Our every wish is the Father’s, and all that we are is the Father’s possession. Our heart and center of love is the Father’s, and if there are those who do not feel this, they are indeed pitiful. 

Even while bleeding on the cross, Jesus knew and held onto such a Father, and thus He said that He was not afraid of death. Rather, we long for that noble and composed character who prayed blessings upon His enemies. We long for that step. Where is the victorious prince who can laugh at the changes in history, the changes in life, and the changes in his own being, today and tomorrow? Father, we long for You.

The historical protagonist, the temporal protagonist, and the future protagonist should not be separated but should appear as one entity, able to convey Your heart to humanity. That time, that world, that garden is what we long for. 

A group that can call You Father must emerge, and a denomination must arise. 

Please allow us to forget everything and prepare to seek that, to devote our hearts and fulfill our responsibilities, and to become sons and daughters who can run without hesitation, regardless of any sacrifice, to stand before the Father. 

Father, what will You do with this 30 million people? What will You do with the 27 that are scattered across this land?
How can we help humanity? We cannot help but worry about the fate of our nation, and when we see that the end of humanity is shrouded in a tragic darkness, we cannot help but feel sorrow. Because I know the historical sorrow of the Father, which cannot be ignored, I convey this heart to ignorant humans, and since I must evoke such feelings, I speak these words, so please accept them. I convey this heartfelt and sorrowful sentiment to prevent unfaithful humans from remaining in their unfaithfulness, so I ask for your acceptance of this prayer, dear Father of love, earnestly hoping and wishing for it. I know that the sorrow of Jesus, who died on the cross, is a historical sorrow, and I miss Jesus, who shed tears of blood on the summit of Golgotha. Now, humanity longs for a figure who can mock history and admonish it as the embodiment of the Father, and I know that heaven also longs for this. I earnestly hope and wish that we may become sons and daughters who wander in search of such a being today and tomorrow. Please do not allow us to be those who are saddened by not being able to walk the path, and let us be those who, after walking the path, still desire to go further and struggle to embrace the joy found after completing the journey. Only then can we learn that we become a cornerstone in the face of the amazing and great providence, so please mobilize us for this purpose today and tomorrow. The world of today and our descendants are destined to be mobilized for this purpose, so please command and lead us. We will go. 

Father! You know all the feelings we want to express, and I earnestly ask that you fulfill our prayers. Please protect us on the remaining rough path. I pray in the name of the Lord. Amen.

If there are sons and daughters who are not worthy before your will, please come personally and admonish them. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for this.

<Prayer (III)> Father! You enjoyed manifesting in silence, and you did not mind appearing in difficult circumstances. At this time, please help us repent of our past faith journey, where we enjoyed rejecting and refusing the earth while living on it. 

The Father, who was glorified in a transcendent realm, is a pitiful, shabby, and sorrowful Father on earth. We have learned through history that you came to us in such a form. 

Now, we should not rejoice in the presence of the Father who has appeared in glory, but we should rejoice in the presence of the Father who is wounded on earth, suffering hardships, and struggling to find true sons. I earnestly hope and wish to stand in such a glorious position.

<Word>
Therefore, stay awake. For you do not know the day or the hour. (Matthew 25:13) The title of the message I wish to deliver from now on is "The Time to Be Awake Like Heaven." I will speak for a moment under this title of the time when we must be awake like heaven.

As you present yourselves before the Father at this time, think about how much of your heart and body is awake, and feel in your hearts what kind of heart and circumstances the Father has in order to awaken you as you listen to this message.

The God Who Is Awake
Whether it is a family, a society, or any nation or ethnic group, we can see that societies or nations that are not awake have perished. Therefore, if there is anything extremely precious to humanity, it is being awake.

So what should we be awake for? We should not be awake by looking at the reality we live in, but we must be awake by looking toward the future that is to come. In other words, we must become people who have a longing heart. When we become such people, we can remain as people of hope or as people of a hopeful nation. Thus, throughout history, those who loved their countries have cried out to their fellow citizens to stay awake while their nations were sinking into darkness and being swept away by the power of death.

Then how much has heaven labored for us, and how much has heaven been awake for us? The extent to which we know this is limited to how much we have labored and how much we have been awake ourselves. However, heaven has not treated humanity according to what you know. Heaven has never forgotten the hope for the ideal of creation since the creation of Adam and Eve. There has not been a single day of rest, nor a moment of slumber. We must understand this.

Heaven was not satisfied merely by creating Adam and Eve and watching them grow. We must not forget that heaven looked at Adam and Eve, who were growing, with concern for their tomorrow, that is, their future, from a position of being awake. Furthermore, we must not forget that heaven has looked at the descendants throughout history from the perspective of the future, from a position of being awake.

So what was the fall? The fall was not knowing the heart of the awake heaven, not knowing the circumstances of heaven, and not knowing the desires of heaven. The heart of the awake heaven! The heart of heaven that wishes to establish a relationship with them! The desire of heaven to enjoy glory together with their future selves! Losing that hope was the fall. Thus, fallen humanity could not see the day of hope that God had wished for. Moreover, they could not establish a deep relationship with God, and furthermore, they lost the embrace of God's love that humanity could not even imagine until now.

Heaven has been concerned for humanity, who have strayed from Your embrace, and has been working to find them again. This is the providence of salvation. When we reflect on ourselves today, who have no relationship with the heart of heaven, the circumstances of heaven, and the desires of heaven, we must realize that we have nothing to repay before the heart, circumstances, and desires of the Father.

Heaven, which was worried that Adam and Eve might fall, has taken on the heart of concern for those who have fallen. And heaven sought to save those who had fallen into the embrace of satan, that is, into the power of death. In other words, God was concerned that humanity might fall, and when they fell, He was concerned for the fallen humanity, wanting to revive Adam and Eve, who were in the place of death, and has come to find us day after day without a moment of slumber for six thousand long years. We must be able to feel this in our hearts during this hour.

Humanity Longing for New Hope and Emotional Shock
What is the desire of humanity? It is the desire to conquer the world beyond their families, beyond their nations, and beyond their states. However, no matter how much one may achieve such desires, if they cannot stand in a position that aligns with the heart of God, the circumstances of God, and the desires of God, they cannot stand before heaven.

Looking back at the historical journey so far, individuals, families, nations, and the world have struggled to find hope over a piece of land. Even now, they are struggling to find a new hope, though they do not know what it is.

However, with how we have lived until now, we cannot find new hope. In other words, we cannot seek new hope with any concepts or attentions derived from historical relationships. This is because there are limitations there. We must anticipate this.

Still, humanity is searching for a situation where the heavenly principles and human principles can be connected from a common standpoint of hope. People from both the East and the West are seeking a situation to build a new ideological world based on one heart, but such a situation has not yet appeared in human history.

We must transcend ethnic boundaries and Eastern and Western cultures, feeling emotionally intertwined and entangled in a fair and uniform situation, yet humanity does not know such a situation.

Thus, humanity feels an inexplicable sense of emptiness. They are longing for some kind of stimulating shock that they do not understand. They are waiting for a new emotional shock that they cannot yet define, but they have not yet received any shock. Therefore, even if we say we have found hope and established relationships through love, if we cannot find a point of emotional unity, we will inevitably disperse at some point.

What does the historical journey of humanity represent? It represents the divine content with which heaven dealt with the human ancestors. This can be said to be the reality of history, which is meant to be shown before humanity. We must understand this.

Now, as people are saying that this is the end time, the hopes that humanity has longed for must retreat, and the circumstances of humanity until now must also retreat, for they cannot establish eternal relationships. The time for this must come.

Moreover, the family-based, social, national, or global foundations centered on one's own heart cannot change into a universal center, a foundation like a rock that no one can move. Therefore, they will inevitably collapse. This is why human hearts are agitated.

The greater the agitation of human hearts, the more urgency they feel, the greater the time of emotional turmoil will come, and when that time comes, there will be hope for humanity.

If such a time does not come, humanity will begin in despair and end in despair. However, if there is a will of heaven for humanity, it is a will that must start with hope and end with hope, and since heaven has the responsibility to fulfill that will, the time when the purpose of history will be achieved will surely come.

However, today, humanity believes that all motivations start from humanity, but that is not the case. Today's society, nations, or the world are not based on any historical relationships. Historical relationships are not connections that started from humanity. They are merely movements that have come along the trajectory of history until a higher relationship and a higher hope are realized.

The Correct Attitude Toward History
When it is said that it is time to wake up, it does not mean waking up from sleep at night. This is a message that is announced in every era. And if there is an ideological world that must be realized in the end times, it is a message that is announced to humanity in every era as they seek that world.

Now, if you have a desire to assert yourself, to claim yourself, and to lead the whole, where does that desire begin? 

You are in a state of slumber. Today, humanity is in a state of slumber. Individuals, families, societies, nations, the world, and even the spiritual world are all in a deep slumber without having met a moment of hope.

This historical relationship will not end in this era as it is, but it must transcend to a new something. If anyone feels that this new something is common, then that new something is the issue.

However, when looking at past history, nations that absolutely insisted on traditional habits have been pushed out of history. We must discard the thoughts we had in the old antique-like times. Today, humanity tends to emphasize the relics of the historical journey because they are walking the path of restoration. This means that what existed in the human world can only be seen as a reflection of God's heart.

Therefore, we who live in the present reality should not be satisfied with antique thoughts but should recognize the precious value of the original ideal through them and be stimulated to entrust ourselves to that precious ideal. Only such individuals can restore the ideals that have been hidden in God's heart since the beginning.

For this reason, we who have reached the end times must not look back at history to find something, but we must settle history and seek that one hour where we can represent the overall ideal hidden in God through ourselves. That hour is the time when both God awakens and humanity on earth awakens.

When the era of restoration has completely passed, we must seek new things. Therefore, if this era is to be called the end, the young men and women living in this era must uproot everything that people have deemed precious until now and cultivate a sincere heart to seek new things, so they can become the workers of the awakened new era. Those who seek new things with open eyes and a struggling heart in this end time will find themselves closer to the path of hope for the future, and they will be able to establish connections with the circumstances of the future and establish relationships with the divine heart that appears in the historical end times.

Then the question here is, what position are you standing in?

Are you standing in a fallen world, a land swept by the power of death, a land that consumes the blood of goodness, where one nation devours another, and where there are historical relationships? If so, you must realize that you have no connection with the world of new hope.

You must go your own way, and I must go my own way, and if there is no clear limit set for you, the flow of history that is swept away by the waves of death will prevent you from establishing a relationship with the new era and will push you into the world of death. Therefore, until now, you had to hold onto this flow of history, but before the judgment seat of the end times, you must transcend it. In other words, after Jesus completed His life of over thirty years and died on the cross, when He was to receive the victory of resurrection, if Jesus had regarded His thirty years of life as important or had prioritized Himself above all else, He would not have been able to resurrect even if heaven wished to resurrect Him.

However, Jesus was able to resurrect because He completely settled all that He had lived until then and was ignited with new hope. And His heart, circumstances, and desires were replaced with those of heaven rather than those of the earth. In that moment, He was able to receive the gift of resurrection.

In the same way, you too will meet such a time of replacement, and those of you who are looking forward to that day must have a firm mental readiness. And no matter what gathering you participate in, you must not base your readiness on the representative of that gathering, but you must establish your own emotional standards through that gathering. Only those who are such can be seen as having a natural environment to awaken.

What We Must Settle
Now, you must move into such a position, but if you acknowledge that you are in a position where you cannot move into such a position today, what should you do? What must you settle here? First, you must understand that you cannot move forward based on human relationships, human circumstances, and human desires.

So what must you establish a relationship with to move beyond? We must not merely discuss the sorrow of human history. We must settle the sorrow of providential history and the sorrow of heaven. Before that, we cannot settle any of this.
because until today, the history of humanity has been a history that has betrayed the will of the heavens, which had placed hope in us countless times. Therefore, we must be able to deeply feel this in our flesh and blood. Only with such a heart can we harbor the hatred for the reality of sin and put an end to the sorrowful history of humanity.

Today, we must reflect on our actions and consider what our actions today testify about the fallen history of humanity. We must also think about how much our actions align with the heavenly actions that establish the providence. We should be able to feel the shock that arises from this difference. When we realize that our actions betray God's heart, God's circumstances, and God's wishes, and that they add to the tears of blood in the heart of heaven, we will come to know that our heart toward heaven is millions of times greater than our heart toward the earth. When that happens, all attachments to the world of death can be severed.

Heaven has been watching over us humans who stand in such a position until now. God has never rested or slumbered for even a single day. The heaven that has witnessed the history of the fall since creation has seen things we cannot see, experienced things we cannot endure, and felt sorrows, frustrations, and grievances that we cannot fathom. Sometimes, He sent true sons and daughters, but even while watching humans kill them, He endured. That Father has never rested for even a single day but has been awake, watching over us. You must be able to feel this. If you live with such a heart, you will not stand in the position of judgment.

Today, your one body, though exceedingly small, is being appealed to by history. The times are appealing to this one body. The world is appealing to this one body. Heaven is crying out for you to awaken.

No one appeared to understand his feelings. They did not even know the path of his 30 years of hard work. Even the followers of John the Baptist, who were in a position to live in the wilderness and bear responsibility for the nation, opposed him.

True faith and practice

Therefore, if humans today cannot analyze the limits of the emotions and sorrows that heaven experiences in the process of fulfilling such true faith and practice, and cannot stand in a position of empathy, they must understand that they are still in a position that cannot be welcomed with both hands in the world of the heavenly ideal.  
For this reason, the footsteps of Jesus were precious. Jesus understood that when his words were established, heaven was established, and when those words were executed, heaven's will was executed. Living in accordance with this standard, Jesus had a great concern for humanity, a great concern for heaven, and a profound feeling of empathy for the sorrows of heaven and earth.  
There are no passages in the Bible where Jesus danced with joy and spoke. Why? Because God has not yet spoken to His children, humanity, from the garden of joy, so even if Jesus had joy in his heart, he could not freely express it with joyful emotions that transcend heaven and earth.  
Jesus' words should have been those that could be introduced with joyful emotions, but the very words spoken were through sorrowful emotions. Therefore, you must now realize the dignity of the words through such emotions.  
If the words that Jesus and I can relate to transcend history and can establish a connection within the realm of reality, then those words are not the words of heaven.  
The essence of a believer and God's desire  
Everyone! Now, if you have a desperate heart to find the path of truth and revive the journey of faith, you must know where the final limit of the faith concept that Jesus spoke with sorrowful emotions lies, and you must go beyond that limit. Jesus had to resolve the sorrows of heaven and the sorrows of humanity, so his heart was filled with immeasurable sorrow. He felt the sorrow of humanity a hundredfold, a thousandfold, and even felt the countless sorrows of God. Therefore, everything must be based on the faith of humanity in the words that emerged through Jesus' sorrowful emotions, so that the severed connection between God and humanity can be reestablished. Establishing such a standard can be said to be the essence of a believer.  
For this reason, Christianity was not a religion of laughter. It was a religion of tears. Therefore, when we know one thing about Jesus, our hearts become heavy, and when we know two things, we cannot help but weep, and as we continue to know, we cannot help but feel that we must become a sacrifice ourselves. When we have faith and practice from such emotions, we can bring the dead back to life.  
No matter how great a merit one has established before heaven, the result of that merit is not due to oneself. It is due to heaven. Then, where does the thread of providence begin? We must understand that the new history of providence has been established and built from the moment the human heart resonates with heaven's sorrow.  
God has urged humanity to walk the path of faith and practice over a long history of 6,000 years. He earnestly wished for all humanity to become such an existence. He desired a substantial being that could present Himself 100 percent before all humanity.  
Heaven is looking for a being that can believe and act infinitely and forget that fact. This is the standard of heaven. He is looking for a being for whom the words to believe are unnecessary and the words to practice are unnecessary. Not only can they establish the words given through Jesus and establish the noun of practice, but they can also be a being that can evoke heaven's emotions. However, there has not been a single person who has transcended the limitations of heaven seeking humanity and practiced.  
The person God is looking for  
Even today, despite the numerous believers in Christianity, where is a single heavenly child who can boast of a journey of practice that transcends such emotional limitations? Where is a heavenly child? The problem lies here. Today, you must be able to dream of establishing the noun of faith, and regardless of any fact, you must be able to regard it as your own and enjoy it freely from eternity to eternity, transcending temporality and historicity. There must be content that God has established a path that serves as the foundation of faith for humanity.  
A being that can forget the laws of faith and loyalty in the world, a being that can forget the value of practice and regard it as more precious than the value of execution, when such a being resonates with heaven's will, only then can heaven finally say, "My son, my daughter." Therefore, the sorrow of not finding true sons and daughters is heaven's sorrow, and it is the sorrow of humanity on this earth. The sorrow of not being able to treat humanity as sons and daughters is heaven's sorrow.  
Today, although we have words to call God the Absolute Being, when we introduce God in this way, there is nothing that can truly resonate emotionally. You must know that there cannot be words that are detached from emotions. Then where is the God with whom words can connect and emotions can resonate? As you embark on the journey of faith, you must confront such questions with a desperate heart, transcending the nouns of faith and practice, and be able to call upon the Father, with your cells and heart unconsciously resonating with Him.  
Heaven is surely looking for a being that can remain in such a physiological state of outcry.  
If there is something that humanity today must weep over, it is the sorrow of the entire humanity for what they could not take responsibility for. We must mourn over our ancestors who have made heaven sorrowful for 6,000 years as traitors and betrayers. Furthermore, we must mourn over our own existence today.  
If we have not even thought about what limitations we have been wandering within from a faith perspective, and we are moving forward, would heaven say, "That is right," or would it say, "How sorrowful"? That heart would be filled with the sorrow of the 4,000 years and the 6,000 years of historical connections. And you must acknowledge that you are in a position where heaven can sigh over you.  
What flowed from the heart that lost faith, lost love, and lost the life of devotion due to humanity's fall was sorrowful emotion. It was an indescribable sorrowful emotion. Therefore, in your faith life, even without realizing it, sorrowful emotions may sprout, and if there are times when sorrow comes in your daily life and surroundings, do you know that it is the time when heaven comes? If there is someone who can hold onto the essence of that sorrow and establish a connection with tears, that person can be revived.  
Humans are meant to establish such connections, but because fallen humanity cannot face heaven in a substantial way, Jesus was sent as a flat protagonist on this earth. Fallen humanity needed the substantial Lord, Jesus. That is why Jesus came to this earth.  
If the Israelite people, who were driven and chased during the 4,000 years of sorrowful history, had been able to hold onto Jesus, who bore heaven's sorrowful emotions, and weep, that nation would have become a nation that shines before the world today. If that had been the case, they would not have lost their nation, lost their sovereignty, lost their land, and become a wandering nation. They would not have become such a nation. Wouldn't that be so?  
The life of Jesus, where sorrow outweighed joy  
The Unification Church was not originally meant to take a rough path. When I see you entering the Unification Church, my heart is more filled with concern than welcome. I look at it with such a heart. Rather than welcoming, I look at it with a hesitant heart.  
The more one feels that heaven's content and circumstances, that is, the earnestness of heaven seeking us humans, have been so earnest, the more they will find it impossible to establish themselves and must deny themselves.  
If one has become a being that can be drawn unknowingly into a realm that cannot be criticized by self-awareness and self-subjectivity, then while feeling the sorrow of that realm, they can only walk this path by taking on a part that can reassure and comfort heaven from a subjective standpoint. Only by doing so can one walk this path.  
If you desire to walk a comfortable path, do not come this way. As I walk, I realize that this step is a lonely step with no friends, a step with no companions, a step that cannot communicate with circumstances, a step that cannot rely on anything, and a step that cannot be trusted. I have come to understand that this is the kind of journey Jesus has undertaken.  
If I were to introduce Jesus today, I would first want to introduce the sorrowful side of Jesus. Jesus, who forgot the time for meals and the time for sleep, holding onto a sorrowful heart, running from village to village, who knew his heart? Who among the people of that time understood his heart and became his friend? Heaven was a sorrowful heaven. The prophets who wanted to represent heaven were also sorrowful sacrifices, and when even Jesus died, the heaven that had a will was a sorrowful heaven.  
Who is that heaven? It turned out to be a Father. Understanding the relationship between God and humanity, it was a relationship between a father and child. Humanity has become a being that does not understand the sorrow of the Father. However, the responsibility to inform humanity of the Father's sorrow, which humanity does not know, does not lie with God Himself. It lies with humanity. That is why prophets came, and Jesus came.  
Jesus is the Prince of Sorrow  
Heaven has long awaited and demanded. The sorrowful journey of faith that Jesus walked, the sorrowful struggle of faith that Jesus fought, those who wish to have the justification of children today must fight in place of that struggle and achieve victory.  
Humanity has not yet had a single day of joy on this earth, nor a single day of glory. When we call upon heaven with sorrowful emotions regarding such circumstances, we will unknowingly come to know that heaven exists.  
As far as I know, Jesus shed many tears that went unnoticed. You must know this fact. Although it appears only in a few places in the Bible, Jesus shed many tears that went unnoticed. He felt a sense of responsibility when looking at the mountains and rivers, and he felt a sense of responsibility when looking at the scattered nations, and he felt a sense of responsibility towards the infinite heaven. When he saw that there were areas where responsibilities were placed but could not be practiced, he felt even greater sorrow, and on top of that, he felt sorrow for not being able to comfort heaven when he should have. He was truly the Prince of Sorrow.  
The Jesus we believe in is not the Prince of all princes, the Prince of glory, or the Prince of victory, but the Prince of Sorrow. We must be able to feel that he is the Prince of sorrow for the sake of the will.  
If I say this, I may be branded as a heretic in Christianity, but it turns out to be true.
Jesus was the prince who could convey the sorrowful heart of heaven, appearing before all people and history for the first time! You must have a moment of overwhelming emotion to connect with Him. Is that all? Jesus was the prince of suffering.

Who were those who took the lead in betraying heaven and cursing it? They were the Jews and the Israelite people, who were established to believe and follow. Heaven would never have prepared the Israelite people for 4,000 years just to have Jesus captured and killed.

When we look at this, we see that Jesus did not completely triumph. He did not achieve perfect victory. Don't you think so? If Jesus' death on the cross was a complete victory, then the day of suffering could not have been more joyful, and that moment on the cross would surely have been the ultimate moment of victory, a moment for all people and all beings to rejoice. Yet, we can clearly see that it was not a moment of joy. That is why, when Mary Magdalene tried to greet Him with a heart full of joy, Jesus stopped her and said not to come. He could not offer glory to heaven, filled with joy alongside His beloved disciples. He could not do that. Because of this, we must understand that Jesus was filled with sorrow, mourning His death, and that His resurrection was achieved with a heart full of sorrow.

We must experience the sorrowful heart of heaven, not knowing where to place our bodies, forgetting the means of our living, and becoming the disheveled companions of Jesus, who was chased from village to village, receiving disdain at every door. 

Jesus was surrounded by His nation, by denominations, by relatives, and even by His beloved disciples. Although He felt the deepest sorrow, He held the heart to give everything to humanity, embracing the heart to believe in humanity.

Because Jesus could not establish a connection with humanity that could feel the sorrowful emotions, He could not fully convey the earnest wishes, heartfelt desires, and circumstances He held in His heart to humanity. You must understand this.

Today, the saints at the end of the day should not claim to be the promised brides who can stand before the prince of the sorrowful Father and the Son, just because they hold onto the words. It does not work that way. It turns out it does not work that way.

Therefore, now you must cry out, "Father! We are fearful of the words, and our actions are lacking." With a heart filled with reverence, tears should come first, and when you think of the Father, your heart should be choked with a yearning feeling. You must understand that you cannot expect anything when you stand before the Father, who has worked hard to lead history, even if you were to become a sacrifice a million times. Thus, your heart must be directed toward heaven, and even as you go, it should feel insufficient, and as you go, it should feel reverent, and as you go, it should be filled with a sense of shame, shedding tears of sorrow. Only then can you become a disciple of Jesus and a bride of Jesus.

We must enter such a realm to understand the words of Jesus, who said, "The foxes have holes and the birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head." (Matthew 8:20) Or, "Capernaum, will you be exalted to heaven? You shall be brought down to Hades." (Matthew 11:23)

When you resonate with such feelings and delve into the words, those words must pierce your bones and flesh as your own words, not just as Jesus' words. Thus, you must have a new ideology, a new determination, and a new resolution, aiming for a new era of purpose, and you must become children of faith who can develop the surrounding environment with such a shocking appearance.

Only then can you stand before Jesus as a bride through the essential world and be a being that can be called a believer.

The Jesus who came to us emphasized the importance of faith, but what did He say? He said, "God is love." He spoke of God in various aspects, such as the God of love, the God of mercy, and the God of righteousness, but in conclusion, He established the definition that God is love. In other words, He made it known that God is a being who seeks true love.

What does the phrase "Love me more than anything" mean? It means that I will believe in you and love you, and heaven treats us that way. Heaven has not spared any time in loving us.

If there are leaders in the church today, and they see the struggling flock, if they do not have the heart to hold onto their lives and weep and wail for them, they will become ministers who are bound by heavenly law. They will be bound by heavenly law. If there is a shepherd who cannot do this, he is a dead shepherd.

What God does is characterized by the heart preceding words. It is said that when the heart is filled with emotion, words burst forth unconsciously, and Satan submits to that. Evil succumbs from such a place. Otherwise, no matter how good the words are, evil will not submit. The heartfelt emotion must manifest itself, feeling the life of humanity at the crossroads of life and death, and not only feeling it as personal pain but also throwing oneself into it, wanting to save them with a heartfelt desire, and only then can salvation be achieved.

When Jesus carried the cross and left, He left behind the command to love. Even on the cross, He did not blame or curse those who were going to the enemy, leaving heaven. 

Because His pity for them surpassed His own painful heart, He could stand in the way of those going to the enemy and raise His hands to pray for them. Only in front of such prayers does Satan submit.

Thus, if one wishes to live for heaven and approach heaven, they should feel guilty when they have more than others in what they eat. If there is someone who can feel guilt about what they wear, what they live in, and who can go with that heart, they will not go hungry, nor will they be chased or cornered. Even if there are times when they are cornered in the world of Satan, those who are seeking the heart of heaven will not be cornered.

Therefore, heaven has told us to "Love me." That love is not the kind of love that you feel with your emotions today or a limited love. It must be a love that can resolve the sorrows of 6,000 years. It is a love that has the sorrowful heart of having to expel Adam from the Garden of Eden, and a love that can weep for lives that are destined for hell.

God's love, even for sinners who deserve punishment, has a legal condition before Satan and heaven. To fulfill that legal condition, He strikes and then weeps, abandons and then holds onto them.

When we look at the history of Israel, the rebellious Israelite people were more than anyone else betrayers and traitors before God. However, heaven abandoned them and then took them back, abandoned them again and took them back. He took back individuals who had been abandoned, and then took back families that had multiplied from there, abandoning and taking back, establishing the Israelite people and developing the world Christianity that can be called the Second Israel today. 

In other words, it has established world Christianity, which can be called the Second Israel.

All believers here must understand God's heart, which even has lingering feelings toward Satan and can forgive Satan. We must know that God is such a being.

Now, knowing that God has such a heart, today you must reflect on the sins of having betrayed heaven and your past life that has fallen short, and not only have a loving heart but also a heart that wants to serve unconditionally and a heart that wants to care unconditionally. From that moment on, you will be the beloved of heaven. 

You must be able to move to a level where you can forget your parents and be unable to remember them.

This was the life of Jesus, who practiced love. If we are to pursue such love, when we see someone who has believed for a long time, we should bow our heads, and when we see someone who has worked hard before heaven, we should want to serve them. If there is no such feeling in your faith life, the connection to heavenly love will be severed.

The love that humanity has held until now is not eternal love, so people are struggling, ready to die in search of that eternal love, using the noun "love." The moment human love collides with the ideal of heavenly love, one feels the sweetness of value that can determine the ownership of the great universe. The moment one touches heavenly love, there can be no lingering feelings even after losing everything. That world is not an illusion; it is not a world of fabricated fantasy, but a world of existential reality.

Such feelings exist within the hearts of humanity today, within the great universe. There are emotions that are revolving toward humanity from the world of heaven that we cannot comprehend. You must not deny this. Jesus came to introduce the essence of love. To introduce this and establish God's love, He had to be filled with a heart that wanted to serve and care for heaven, which had worked hard for thousands of years on behalf of humanity.

Until now, the world of faith has been like this. First, it is the world of faith, and second, it is the world of love. The world of love speaks of the world of bride and groom. Now, what kind of era is ahead? It is the era of serving. However, one must pass through the process of faith and the process of love to enter the era of serving.

To practice such love, even if adversity comes today and tomorrow, it was the life of Jesus, who had to give and serve endlessly. Jesus once said to the Pharisees, "You are like whitewashed tombs," and cursed them, but He wanted to care for them infinitely and wanted to support them infinitely, and because they did not understand that heart, He spoke those words.

Today, we cannot find those who live for others. We truly cannot find those who live for others. This nation cannot become a nation that lives for others. It has no ideology to live for others. Because it has no ideology to care for this nation in the past, present, and future, we must understand that it is in conflict with the will of heaven, which wants to care for us.

The same goes for you. There must be a heart that can automatically manifest itself to care for the past, present, and future. If one is centered on oneself, saying, "I will succeed and make a name for myself," that is the path of fall. That is the path of fall.

If one stands in the position of a sovereign, they are not someone who should be exalted; they are someone who must give for the entirety of 30 million people.

God's desire - Restoration of Heaven

In this realm, you who are seeking the world of heart must not believe for yourselves. Let us abandon the concept of going to heaven, the concept of what I will do. 

Jesus did not think of going to heaven for himself. He had the faith concept of believing for the universe, believing for the nation, and further believing for God. This is not a fabricated word. It was indeed so.

What I do is not for myself but for humanity, for the world, and on behalf of the Father. How refreshing is this! 

When I love, I do not love for my own sake, but I love for the nation, I love for humanity, I love for God, and I care for heaven and earth. Therefore, our service must also be for humanity and for heaven. While serving, we must have a heart of gratitude and a determination to practice.

We must be able to love with our hearts and serve with our bodies, and while serving with our hearts, we must be able to express gratitude through our lives. If we walk the path of faith with the concept of going beyond ourselves to believe, love, and serve, then Satan will never be able to invade. No matter how strong the hand of temptation from Satan may be, it cannot touch such believers.

Then what is heaven's desire? It is to restore the lost heaven. It is to restore the lost parents. It is to restore the lost children.

I have also come to realize that humanity, which has lived with the thoughts of Satan until now, has been in a deluded state, and that the foundation of restoration that must be resolved by crossing the peak of death has now arrived at our doorstep.

Now we must become the sons and daughters of the heavenly Father and be able to call you our true Father. May the heart of the Father’s love for humanity penetrate our hearts, so that we can overcome any adversity, any sorrow, and any discomfort. Father, I earnestly hope and wish for your guidance and leadership.

Among your sons and daughters who are present here today, are there any who do not feel gratitude for having life? If they are moved and feel something in the words, please ignite the flame of life and raise the history of resurrection. 

May this time be one that pursues the heavenly ideals, and may this hour be one that can connect with the heart of the Father while pioneering the historical environment of today. 

May the words conveyed become the standard of our hearts and our living standards, and may they lead these hearts and become a stimulating standard in their lives, always being a living word that can rectify the unjust, and may you work so that it can move their hearts and bones. 

At this time, please comfort those who are weeping and appealing before you in lonely circumstances, and extend your blessing to the countless humanity that worships before you, I earnestly ask this in the name of the Lord. Amen.

Our hearts and bodies are created in your image, so we earnestly hope and wish to become sons and daughters who fully resemble you, Father. 
Father! Humanity does not realize that your sorrowful heart is lingering on this earth, nor do they know that the traces of your tears from heaven are permeating the footprints of human history. They do not realize that the endless sighs of heaven are swirling around our hearts and bodies, and we must acknowledge that we have become the descendants of fallen humanity who cannot stand before heaven or receive heaven's trust. 
Father, there is no one on this earth to gather your tears, no one to hold your sorrow and comfort you, and no one to guard the path you walk. Therefore, if there is sorrow on this earth, it is a sorrow that is deeply felt in heaven; if there is sadness, it is a sadness that is deeply felt in heaven; if there is resentment, it is a resentment that is deeply felt in heaven. 
Thus, the humans living on this earth are in a fate where they cannot help but become offerings of sorrow, and they are in a fate where they cannot help but cross over into a place of lament. 
In despair, it is time to cry out to heaven with the final voice, "Father, please help us." And it is time to cry out, "Father, please come to humanity with a heart of love." So that we may become your sons and daughters who can be offered as sacrifices worthy of your glory, we earnestly hope and wish for this, beloved Father.

Even if we encounter trials and tribulations, we have already resolved to become offerings for you, so please do not let us become sons and daughters who lose that heart to Satan. Our bodies and hearts have already been entrusted to you, and we have offered them to you, so whether we live or die, may we be taken and offered as yours.
