<Message> The words we have read are the final words of curse that arose from the sorrowful heart of Jesus Christ, who thought about the path he must take soon, and the hope and expectation he had for Israel were as earnest and great as his sorrowful heart in not being able to establish his will before them. 
Today, I will speak on the theme of "The Many Sorrows of the Father." 
The Sorrowful Humanity, The Sorrowful History, The Sorrowful God
Today, we long for a happy life. Furthermore, we yearn for a land of freedom in our hearts. However, we are well aware through our daily lives that what we hope for and yearn for in our hearts is in conflict with the reality in which we live today. 
Even during a single day, we should have something in our hearts that can manage and dominate the conflicting elements, but because we do not have that, we are unable to go where our hearts wish to go. We also feel that what we desire in our hearts does not easily translate into action. 
In the midst of this, we feel that we do not have the ideology that can govern ourselves, nor do we have any concerns that can organize our environment. We have been living with great hopes and dreams, but on the other hand, we always feel a sense of sorrow in our hearts. We are living such sorrowful lives today, just as we did yesterday. 
These sorrowful groups are coming together to form a nation and a world. We know through the course of history that this sorrowful self is being extended into society, nations, and the world. 
It is not only humanity that is in a sorrowful history. Because humanity is walking a sorrowful path, everything that belongs to humanity is also in this sorrowful environment. 
Furthermore, if there is a Creator who governs humanity and wishes to restore an ideal world, we must understand that even He cannot find joy when facing this earth due to the sorrowful history caused by humanity. 
The more sorrowful things we have within ourselves, the more sorrowful facts that occur in our society, and the more sorrowful events that take place throughout the world, we cannot help but think that these sorrowful matters do not begin and end with humanity alone, but rather affect the divine realm that governs history beyond this earth. And indeed, this is the truth. 
We cannot deny that there is a God who has been holding and governing humanity for 6,000 years since the fall. To end the sorrowful life of 6,000 years, there will be a stark contrast between the sorrowful work of heaven and the sorrowful matters that seep into your hearts today. 
If a true human being arises who can eliminate all the sorrowful elements of the human world, resolve what heaven has been sorrowful about, and build a nation of peace on earth, they must go through all the sorrowful adversities of their own personal history and the sorrowful moments of humanity, along with the heart of heaven. 
If they cannot do this, there can be no peaceful world, no world of happiness, and no garden of freedom that is free from the encroachment of sorrowful history in the human world. 
Examine your own hearts and ask yourselves. Who am I, and for whom and for what purpose am I wandering? What answers come from that question? If you cannot find a certain answer with a solid belief and value, the more serious that question is, the more your lamenting heart will be proportionate to it. 
The Divine Providence to Resolve Sorrow
If we are in a position to settle the grievances of history and the twists of heaven's providence, what resolve, what form, and what attitude can you take to answer that question? If heaven approaches humanity with a heart full of grievances, unable to resolve the sorrowful feelings of history— and indeed, this is the case—who will be able to resolve the grievances of heaven? We must understand that the cause of this sorrowful twist lies not with heaven, but with humanity. 
If humanity does not realize that they are in a position to resolve these grievances and cannot clarify the twists, the history of grievances will continue to revolve and pass through ages and centuries, becoming a history that is estranged from heaven's providence. 
If heaven exists, it will seek one person who can block this history and resolve the grievances of heaven and humanity. Heaven has fought until now to establish that one person. It is certain that it has governed history until today for that one person to serve heaven. Now is the time for us to reflect on this aspect. Heaven has promised to send that one person, and that one...
To raise a person, He has fought an infinite battle and has gone through an infinite history of suffering to save that one person. However, throughout history, there has been no one who has accompanied that one person, nor has anyone held onto that one person, which is why Heaven still harbors a deep resentment. We are destined to fight along the path of Heaven's resentment. We must think about this once again.

God is a being filled with such sorrow. God cannot express His sorrow before humanity, nor can He convey His grief to humanity. This deep-seated resentment does not originate from Heaven; it comes from humanity. Therefore, Heaven has carried this sorrow and has led human history, establishing eras and striving to pioneer the future while still harboring feelings of resentment. We must recognize that such a Heaven exists.

Thus, God's will is to establish a figure who can resolve Heaven's sorrow, and it is His will to save that one existence. In this historical end time, you must have a sincere desire for me, for us, and for this nation to be granted the grace to establish that day when we can resolve Heaven's sorrow. Furthermore, since God is filled with sorrow, we must not forget that we, as humanity, are indebted to serve the God who is filled with sorrow and to help relieve that sorrow.

You must feel that Heaven is still working tirelessly to save humanity, to relieve humanity's sorrow, and to remove all the twists of human grief. If there is someone who feels this, they will turn back from their path, organize their living, settle their past life, and hold onto the sorrowful heart. It is time to feel this shock in our hearts. If we cannot feel this, we must prepare ourselves to face a day of judgment filled with deep-seated resentment.

Today, we must remember that we are the sons and daughters who bear the heavenly mission to accompany Heaven, which is filled with sorrow, and to resolve the sorrows of this world. We must recognize that, as descendants of fallen humanity, we have the responsibility and duty to fight for the hearts of many fathers who are filled with sorrow.

The Reason Jesus Must Return

Therefore, after humanity's fall, Heaven warned through 4,000 years of history, selecting a chosen people and promising them, "I will send you a leader, your master, the prince of peace, the prince of freedom, and the prince of happiness." Thus, Heaven sent that one promised figure, who is the protagonist of happiness, the protagonist of peace, and the protagonist of freedom, capable of resolving Heaven's sorrow and introducing Heaven's blessings.

That promised figure appeared after a long history, but the chosen people of Israel could not accompany Him, nor did they welcome Him or live according to His will. Because they could not unite according to His will and fight to establish Heaven's purpose and relieve God's sorrow, the sorrowful history has continued to this day.

So who is that prince of peace, that prince of happiness, that prince of freedom? It was Jesus Christ, who bore the sorrowful heart of humanity throughout the 4,000 years of history after the fall. Jesus, who was to bear the responsibility of 4,000 years of human history and 4,000 years of God's providence, came with the historical and heavenly sorrow.

What process did Jesus have to go through to relieve that sorrow? He had to go through a process of grief and a process of suffering. Only after that could the sorrow be relieved and a time of joy come. Therefore, you must not forget that Jesus, who came to this earth, experienced the sorrow of 4,000 years of history more than anyone else and bore the pain of suffering.

Today, Christian believers believe in Jesus Christ. They believe Him to be the King of kings, the only begotten Son of Heaven, their Savior, the prince of peace, and the prince of happiness who introduces happiness to them. 

Before recognizing Jesus in such a positive light, you must first understand that He is the prince of sorrow, the prince of suffering, and the prince who bears the sorrow of all humanity.

That sorrowful heart of Jesus Christ, for whom was it? It was for the humanity of that time and for God, who holds onto humanity. That sorrowful heart is the heart He brought from Heaven, a heart He brought to convey to humanity.

However, no one has stepped forward to inherit that sorrowful heart and to fight against evil to relieve that sorrow. Therefore, we must understand that not only was Jesus' sorrow great, but God's sorrow, who sent Him, was even greater.

Thus, the history of the earth is filled with resentment, this era is filled with resentment, and we ourselves are filled with resentment. Therefore, we want to remove the deep-seated resentment of history, the resentment of this era, and our own resentment, but we feel that we are in a position where we cannot do so by ourselves.

Thus, we are destined to meet a protagonist who can take responsibility for the entirety of that deep-seated resentment. Therefore, the dying Jesus, who resurrected and ascended, must come to this sorrowful earth to resolve the twists of this sorrowful heart. That is the Second Coming.

God's Sorrow and the Faith of the End Time Saints

We say that God is love. Therefore, we understand that God has been loving humanity for 6,000 years. 

If there is sorrow, there is no sorrow greater than the sorrow that seeps through the heart of love, and if there is suffering, there is no suffering greater than the suffering that seeps through the heart of love. Furthermore, if there is joy, there is no joy greater than the joy that seeps through the heart of love.

Then, if Heaven is love, has the loving God been joyful? No, He has not. The Heaven that faces fallen humanity, the Heaven that loves humanity, has not had a day of joy until today. We must understand that. 

Because He has a heart of love, the greater the desire to save humanity, the greater the sorrow that seeps into that heart. There is no one on this earth who feels the heavenly suffering that is filled with love.

Humanity knows that God is love and that He is the subject of love, but they do not know the heart of suffering that God bears on behalf of humanity.

What must the saints at the end time understand? Having known the loving God, we must understand the heavenly sorrow that seeps into that heart, and we must understand the heavenly suffering that seeps into that heart. The time has come for this.

Even if heavenly joy through love is granted on this earth, that joy cannot be given to the saints who are hoping for joy as we believe today. Why? Because that joy is a happiness that must be bestowed through history, a hope that has been promised before history. This happiness and hope do not arise beyond me; they arise along with the history that leads me.

Therefore, if we speak of God's love, those who have the heart to hold onto the loving God today are those who hold onto the sorrow that seeps into God's heart and the suffering that seeps into the heart of love. Only such individuals can receive the happiness introduced through Heaven's love as their inheritance.

Then what is God's sorrow? It is not that there are no people who believe in God. It is not that there are no people who recognize God. If there is sorrow in the loving God, it is that there are no people who recognize the sorrow that seeps into God's heart of love, nor are there people who recognize the suffering that seeps into the heart of love. This is the sorrow and resentment of God that you must understand.

If the end time comes when we must resolve the sorrow of humanity and relieve the heavenly sorrow, what kind of protagonists must we become? We must become those who can hold onto the sorrowful heart and the suffering heart on behalf of Heaven and love humanity. We must start from having such a heart. It should not be about asking, "Please hold onto me and love me," but rather, "Please hold onto humanity and love humanity."

If there is someone who moves into action unknowingly through such a deep-seated heart, they can be seen as one who bears witness to the heavenly sorrow in the human world and one who has experienced heavenly suffering.

The Sorrow of Jesus and the Sorrow of God

Therefore, Jesus, who came to relieve Heaven's sorrow, did not appear with happiness, nor did He appear with freedom. He appeared as the greatest among sinners while being in the highest position before God. Is there anything sadder than this?

Though He is the prince of Heaven who could make all of Heaven rejoice, on earth, He lived as the prince of oppression, the prince of persecution, and the prince who was disappearing. There is no sorrow greater than the sorrow of Jesus.

Who could be sadder than Jesus, who could not fulfill His dignity, His position, and His mission and silently disappeared in the face of adversity? Jesus was rejected by the Israelite people, whom Heaven had chosen after 4,000 years of effort. He was persecuted by the Jewish sect that had long loved Him to fulfill the providential will.

It did not stop there. He was rejected by His beloved people and persecuted by His beloved disciples. If Jesus had human resentment at that moment, He could only have cursed them. He came for the nation, but the sect betrayed Him, and He came for His kin and chosen ones, yet He was betrayed by them as well.

In such a position, if Jesus had harbored resentment and cursed them, He could have expressed a curse that words could not convey. Yet, Jesus held onto the sorrowful heart of those who had suffered through history and had to forget Himself and worry for them. We must understand this situation of Jesus.

Jesus knew that He was the prince of building the kingdom of Heaven, but that was a later matter. Jesus was the prince of sorrow, who came to remove all the sorrows of the world and to experience the heartfelt sorrow and deep-seated resentment of the many prophets and sages who had longed for goodness and purpose throughout history. He was the prince of sorrow who had to bear all the burdens of humanity, who were groaning under the dominion of darkness and Satan, not knowing where to go.

Internally, He had to take responsibility for the sorrowful heart, and externally, He had to bear the burden of suffering, resolving this before Satan and establishing a foundation for victory before Heaven. This is what we must understand.

And we must also understand that when such Jesus came to this earth and lived in such sorrow and suffering, God's heart, which looked upon Him, was filled with even more sorrow than Jesus' sorrow and more pain than Jesus' pain.

Look. God created Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden and wished for them to grow up beautifully. However, because Adam and Eve fell in the garden of permitted freedom, in the world of the permitted ideal, they lost that peace and happiness they were meant to share with Heaven and were cast out of the Garden of Eden. This fact was an immeasurable sorrow for God.

We must understand that Heaven had to witness Adam and Eve, who were meant to live eternally in harmony with God, being violated by Satan and being taken away by Satan. 

To change this sorrowful history of humanity that has lasted for 4,000 years, Jesus came to resolve that lamentable history and to build a world of happy restoration. But where did the nation that was to receive Jesus go? Where did the John the Baptist, who was to uphold Him, go? Where did the disciples, who were to fulfill the providence, go? They all left.

The selection of the Israelite people was not to lead Jesus through a path of sorrowful suffering. If He had been sent to die, there would have been no reason to choose the Israelite people as the chosen ones for 4,000 years. The nation that was to receive Jesus, the sect that was to uphold Him, and the apostles who were to be faithful before Jesus all abandoned Him. What do you think Jesus felt when He saw them all leaving?

Though He came for the land, He had to leave the land; though He came for the nation, He had to leave the nation; though He came for the sect, He had to leave the sect. This was the sad reality of Jesus.

Thus, there were many times when Jesus turned His steps toward the Mount of Olives. As He walked, what kind of prayer did Jesus offer to Heaven? His concern was greater for the sorrow of the God who sent Him than for His own sorrow in His unjust position.

It was God's will to send Jesus to live well with the nation and to lead the nation to become an ideal nation for all, but when that path was blocked, Jesus was in a position to offer a heartfelt prayer before Heaven. He did not pray to escape His own suffering but to comfort the greater sorrow of the God who sent Him. This is what we must understand.

As Jesus went to the cross, He said, "My Father, if it is possible, let this cup pass from me; nevertheless, not as I will, but as You will." (Matthew 26:39) He knew that the sorrow and resentment of the Father, who had to push Him into such a position, were greater, so He prayed, "Not as I will, but as You will." This heart allowed the historically sorrowful heart of Heaven and the mission-driven sorrow of Jesus to become one through Jesus Himself. We must understand that this moment was realized at the moment of His death on the cross.

Since the fall of Adam 4,000 years ago, the death of Jesus was an event that further intensified the sorrow of the Father’s heart filled with resentment, but Jesus did not lament His own death; He manifested God's suffering. Thus, He has paved the way to relieve that sorrow up to the present day.
is the essence. Thus, it has come to pass through a history of 2,000 years until today. 
The first Israel was completely shattered by the death of Jesus, but the path of reorganization centered on the resurrected Jesus is the path of the second Israel's chosen people. Therefore, the time has come to unify the Christians scattered across the world, who are the chosen people of the second Israel today. 
In the past, the first Israel boasted of its chosen status, but the Christians of the second Israel scattered across the world must rise up to promote the ideology of the second Israel and construct the welfare of Canaan, which is heaven. 
God has mobilized the second Israel scattered across the world to establish the rights of the common people and has sought out Israel, which has the authority to go through the history of judgment. 
Then, when will the sorrowful heart of heaven, which has borne such a painful history, be released? The first Israel, which once boasted of its chosen status, was led to ruin and trampled by Satan, but the second Israel, which can boast of the rights of the common people, must drive out the world of Satan. Only then can the sorrowful history be resolved through us believers today, and we must understand that we can establish a point of reconciliation before God, who has guided this sorrowful history, and before Jesus and the Holy Spirit, who have gone through countless twists and pains for 2,000 years since the death of Jesus. 
We must now break free from the sorrowful history at the end of history and, transcending the world, penetrate the sorrowful heart of the Father and experience the sorrow and pain in His heart. We must become the sons and daughters of heaven who are determined to deliver the final blow to the countless Satans that have caused the historical grievances and deep-seated resentments. 
To settle accounts with Satan, the author of historical grievances, we must recognize that it is Satan who has created this world, who has led this world, and who has established the realities of this present age. Therefore, today’s saints must carry the heavenly sorrow and pain in their hearts and, with the rights of the common people, move to settle accounts with Satan, the author of historical grievances. We must understand that heaven desires to see one movement, one nation, and one sovereignty appear on this earth. 
What must we do to become such individuals? As we learn the Principle of Restoration in the Unification Church, we must engage in a faith life that resonates with God's heart. We must experience God not just as a father in name but as a real and tangible father. From that position, we must be able to empathize with the sorrowful heart of God, who looked upon the fall of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden and was infinitely sorrowful. 
Next, we must empathize with the heart of God, who was infinitely sorrowful when Cain killed Abel. After that, we must feel the sorrowful heart of God as we look upon the countless ancestors who were sent as responsible figures with heavenly missions throughout the ages, from Noah after 1,600 years to Abraham after 400 years, to Moses after another 400 years, and finally to Jesus. 
We must also empathize with the heart of God, who has guided the providence through 4,000 years and 6,000 years of history, during which the representative figures of God's providence have mourned. All people living on this earth today must mourn on their behalf. 
With such a heartfelt determination, we must empathize with the grievances that have caused pain and sorrow throughout history and resolve the historical anger and the emotional anger of God. If we do not possess such a heart, we cannot be established as the hope of the end times that Jesus seeks and cannot take our place as the bride. 
Therefore, if there are true believers among the saints of the end times today, they will encounter moments that immerse them in an infinitely sorrowful heart that they may not even recognize, and they must overcome those moments. 
It is the end times when we must resolve the historical, epochal, and future grievances. Thus, as we approach these end times, we must weep with the sorrowful history, weep with the times, and shed tears for the future. 
When we forget our own happiness and find ourselves in a position where we must bear the sorrow and pain of humanity, the joy of heaven will be revealed through such people. 
We believe that God is love. Countless scriptures teach that God is love. So how much have you engaged in a faith life that resonates with the heart of love through those words? Have you looked upon the many historical sufferings with the heart of heaven, worried about the many intentions, and contemplated the many sorrows of God? Have you realized that in the heart of our heavenly Father, who calls humanity to come forth with the heart of love, there is more sorrow and pain in seeking us than there is joy in welcoming us? We must empathize with such a heart. 
Father! Looking at heaven, I am indescribably sorrowful. When I think of Your will and look upon humanity, who should be infinitely sorrowful, I am indescribably pained. This was the heart of loyalty that Jesus had toward heaven. Because God should not have sorrow and pain, if there is joy, let it be Yours, and let sorrow and pain be entrusted to me. This was the essence of the gospel that Jesus sought to establish, that we must understand. 
We have struggled to find the blessings of heaven until now. Then who will pave the way to find the blessings of heaven and introduce the blessings of heaven? Who will lay the foundation for this? Who will be responsible for paving this way? There is no way to pave this path with joy. 
The history of Christianity is a history of sorrow and pain. Christianity is a religion of sorrow and pain. Not only Christianity but any religion that carries the name of the Way must move in this manner. 
Have you ever empathized with the moment of embracing historical sorrow and the sorrow of humanity? Have you ever empathized with the moment of embracing historical pain and the pain of humanity? If you have not, then you must do so, even if it means dying, even if it means dying. That is hell. The place of sorrow, that is hell. 
Therefore, the saints on earth must break free from the sorrow of hell and step over the pain of hell. Only then can they taste the joy of heaven before they die. This is the heavenly principle. 
Who is the one to save the nation? It must be one who deeply feels the sorrow of the nation and the pain of the nation. Who is the one to save the world? Today, the advanced nation is not America. Do not rely on them. They can be the servants of the world but cannot rule it. If they are a nation that knows the sorrow of the world, they do not know. If they are a nation that knows the pain of the world, they do not know. If they do not know the sorrow and pain of the world, they cannot rule the world. 
If we speak of a loyal subject of a single nation, he is one who seeks to bear all the sorrows and pains of that nation. <Words> The title I wish to speak to you about is "The New Self and the Heaven Where He Can Live." I will briefly speak on this title, "The New Self and the Heaven Where the New Self Can Live."

The ultimate hope of humanity and the reality we face
There are many people living on the earth, but no one can confidently say that they possess heaven in their hearts. And the ideal world that humanity longs for and seeks out must surely be the heaven that has just been mentioned.

In today's world, many desire to be in a good and blessed position, but very few can say they have lived well or have been blessed. When we look at this situation, we cannot deny that our lives on earth are not a heavenly life but rather the opposite. My own self, standing on this boundary, is in a position that must seek to go toward heaven. We cannot deny that we are in a position where we must find a place to live in such a realm. Thus, our hearts are searching for a better ideal, and our bodies are also seeking a better resting place.

However, today, throughout history, there has not yet appeared a place, a way of life, or a social organization that can confidently be presented as the best, a place where the true heart of humanity can resonate.

Therefore, even though there is a world of hope that our hearts desire, we are in a position where we cannot escape the undesirable living environment and are living with difficulties today. Tomorrow will likely be the same. In the course of our lives, we are in a position where we must live lamenting and complaining within the realm of hope.

So, when will this self, who is in such an environment, be able to overcome and reach the garden of hope, the garden of ideals, and the world of happiness? Or when can we live centered on what we desire? This is a question we must reconsider today, and it is one of the most pressing issues that humanity must readdress and resolve.

However, we cannot stand by regarding this issue. Furthermore, even if this is a difficult problem to realize, we are in a fate that cannot sever it from our inner world through our own lives.

Were we born in the garden of happiness?
We were born on this earth. However, whether it was good or bad to be born with a life on this earth, we have not even thought about it. Many people do not think about whether living like this in reality is a true life or not. Moreover, we are in a position where we must eventually shed our physical bodies and die. We are well aware that as individual beings, we are in a position where we must cross the threshold of death.

Then, whether one’s death is a true death and whether one dies in a true place or not is a matter that is directly related to you and is connected through your life. We must not forget that we are in a realm where we must conclude what we have started.

While many may take pride in being born of their parents' bloodline, if there is one who possesses the heart of a true parent, they must look upon their children with a sigh. Also, just because a child lies in the cradle of happiness at the moment of birth does not guarantee that their life will be happy. As long as that child cannot resonate with the heart of joy before the parents, the parents themselves will inevitably experience sorrow before they can feel joy.

If we acknowledge that their birth did not come from the garden of happiness, then their life will be the same, and their death will also be the same. We must keep in mind that we are living in such a realm. Have you ever hoped for a true life? Do you have the ability to sing the value of true life and triumphantly cross the death you will eventually face? If asked, no one would be able to answer "yes."

For this reason, these individuals and all humanity are in a fallen realm and possess a fate that must lament. Therefore, we are not in a normal world of the heart but in an abnormal world, in an abnormal environment. Because of this, throughout the entirety of life, from the day we are born until the time we die, no one can establish the noun "happiness."

Thus, we must recognize that the happiness, ideals, and hopes that humanity desires do not have any relation to you today. Therefore, the reason my heart is not happy is that I have not become one who can rejoice in myself.

If I had the heart that has achieved the reality of hope, I would rejoice in that fulfillment, but today I do not have such joy. If I had achieved the ideological reality, I would be in a position to stand confidently and command all things to follow me, but today I do not stand in such a position.

The human who should have true ideals does not have true ideals, and the human who should live in a happy environment has lost the garden of happiness. We should have been those who sing of freedom and peace and, furthermore, should have been those who glorify the entirety of happiness that permeates our hearts before the Creator, but we have not become such humans. In light of this, we must first recognize that there is nothing more pitiful and nothing more sorrowful than this.

For this reason, Jesus came to bear all the burdens of four thousand years of history, to take on the entire responsibility of the ancestors who came and went throughout four thousand years, and to carry all the ideals and hopes that humanity held during the historical journey of four thousand years, and to bring the ideals of happiness and heaven. Thus, Jesus must be the friend among our hearts, the center of our hearts, the center of our entire lives, and the center of our hopes, ideals, and even the center of life and death.

And Jesus must have left behind the noun "happiness" on this earth.

Heaven has governed for four thousand long years to restore humans who remain in this realm of lamentation and those who remain in the unhappy realm of death, so that they can once again have new hopes and feel happiness in the new realm of heavenly ideals.

To fulfill this providence
So, what kind of strategy must be brought forth to fulfill this providence? One must take the position of setting apart a holy person. Because people living on this earth cannot connect with heaven as they are, heaven has chosen a chosen people to establish a connection with humanity throughout the historical journey.

We know well the historical process of providence where a chosen people were selected among the chosen people. Choosing Noah was such, choosing Abraham was such, and choosing Moses was likewise.

God's heart was to conclude four thousand years of history by establishing one Jesus, and through this Jesus, to fulfill all historical resolutions. Therefore, God was in a position where He could not do without this Jesus, and the chosen Israelite people who were coming forth with the historical providence were also in a position where they could not do without Jesus. It was not only the chosen people. The humanity of the world at that time was also in a position where they could not do without Jesus. Furthermore, all things that existed at that time, that is, any creature connected from heaven to earth, were also in a position where they could not do without Jesus.

If there is no heaven, that is one thing, but if there is heaven, then for the one reality that humans desire, or to achieve a happy environment, there must be a principled standard established from which to begin. 

Just as no problem can be solved without a formula, if there is no principled standard that can introduce the historical grievances to the hearts of humanity, then no matter how much happiness there is in heaven, it cannot relate to humanity, and no matter how much ideology and life there is in heaven, it cannot relate to humanity. For this reason, to be able to substitute God's heart, to substitute God's happiness, and to substitute the entire ideology of heaven, heaven has guided the Israelite people to embrace such a heart and uphold such an ideology. Therefore, we must understand that God sent Jesus after four thousand years of providence to build the garden of happiness and the garden of goodness that could be connected to heaven.

Who is Jesus?
Then, who is Jesus? Throughout the four thousand years of historical journey, no one could introduce God's joy, but through Jesus' coming, God's joy could finally be introduced, and the garden of happiness that God allows could be built. We must understand that Jesus was a historically new existence. One aspect of Jesus was the reality that the ancestors had hoped for, and it was the existence of hope that the ancestors had fought to find, which the Israelite people at that time had to recognize.

Moreover, Jesus himself was the being that revived the hopes of the ancestors, the being that represented the land that was deeply embedded in God's heart, the being sent by God to realize the heavenly ideals that God longed for in the human world, and our representative being who could build the garden of happiness before humanity. This is what the Israelite people of that time had to recognize. However, they did not know. Therefore, we must understand that although Jesus came to this earth, he could not become the protagonist of the new world, could not possess the people of the new world, could not pioneer the life of the new world, and could not establish the society and nation of the new world.

Today, the earth we live on is a fallen world. Everything in this fallen world cannot become the reality that God intended, and therefore cannot appear as a form that can please God. The life, environment, and nation we live in today are environments, societies, nations, and worlds that cannot resonate with God's heart as they are. We must understand that heaven is looking upon this world with a declaration of judgment.

So now, what is heaven longing for? Heaven longs for something new.
that can connect with God's heart. Therefore, Jesus came to this earth to create individuals who could walk the historical path with the heart that could resonate with God's heart and historical sentiment. Although the Jewish people expected to follow God's history, they could not follow with their hearts. They followed the providence of God but could not embrace God's heart.

To enter into a relationship with God, one must come forth with a life that emerges through God's heart.
278   A New Me and the Heaven Where He Can Live

Our Faith Attitude in the End Times
What kind of filial sons and daughters would there be? A person who is joyful in front of their parents because they are happy in life is not necessarily a filial son or daughter. Then who was Jesus? He was the new reality of resurrection that could exchange for 4,000 years of history. For Whom Did Jesus Live?
Jesus was born as a new being for the first time in human history, but he lived a pitiful life.

He lived for the pitiful nation. The resurrected Jesus has been working until now to bring the dead us back to life. This is the history of 2,000 years since Jesus. Whose life was his 30 years of life? It was not a life lived for Jesus himself, but a life lived for God and fallen humanity. 
Furthermore, for whom has God, who sent Jesus, been working until now? God has never lived for himself. He has been working to revive these fallen and dead people. 
So, what is the end time? Since Jesus could not live for himself, humanity must grant him a time to establish himself. Since God has not been able to move for himself until now, we must grant him a time to move for himself. That time is the end time. 
Until now, God has not been able to live for himself to save fallen humans, the dead. Jesus also could not live for himself throughout 2,000 years of history. God has been working for 6,000 years to restore a new day to embrace and revive dead humanity.

Love me more than anyone else
Jesus said, "Do not think that I came to bring peace to the world. I did not come to bring peace but a sword." (Matthew 10:34) This was an astonishing declaration. The people of Israel understood the Messiah to be a king of peace, a savior to atone for the sins of all humanity, yet Jesus made this surprising declaration. It was a declaration that could apply to every aspect of existence: national, social, familial, and personal.

Then He said, "For I have come to set a man against his father, a daughter against her mother, and a daughter-in-law against her mother-in-law; and a man's enemies will be those of his own household." (Matthew 10:35) Can such words exist? Furthermore, He stated that anyone who loves their father or mother more than Him is not worthy of Him, and anyone who loves their son or daughter more than Him is not worthy of Him. "And whoever does not take up their cross and follow me is not worthy of me." (Matthew 10:37-38) He also said, "Whoever finds their life will lose it, and whoever loses their life for my sake will find it." (Matthew 10:39) From a contemporary perspective, these words seem contradictory.

Although 2,000 years have passed since Jesus, if we understand that the time of His providence was a time of culmination and gathering, then the words proclaimed in that era must eventually be released in the end times. All the words in the 66 books of the Bible that have not yet been revealed must be released in the end times. The entangled world must be untangled, and any entangled sovereignty, society, family, or individual must be released in the end times. Then, we must consider how we will be affected by this.

Jesus said, "Love me more than anyone else." This was a revolutionary statement. It did not involve concepts related to one's parents, beloved children, or spouses. Heaven acknowledges that this world is a fallen world. Where did this history begin? It began with Adam and Eve forming a blood relationship centered around Satan. The history started based on the affection established with the archangel. Heaven cannot accept nations and peoples that are breeding evil centered around evil. This is the anguish of Heaven.

We know about the Noahic judgment, where only Noah and his eight family members were saved while the entire world was swept away. Why did Heaven leave only Noah and his family after 120 years of building the ark, while judging all of humanity and everything that had proliferated at that time with water? Heaven wanted to judge humanity and all creation that had received the blood of Satan, and needed a lineage that could connect with God's heart, one that could establish a blood relationship centered around God. It was not a lineage connected to Satan but one that could connect with God's love. Thus, Heaven destroyed all of humanity and left only Noah's family.

Jesus came as the savior of all humanity, but what kind of savior was He? He was not a savior who came to promote any ideology. He was not a savior who came to create a happy environment by pioneering social conditions. So what kind of savior was He? He was a savior who could transfer the lives of all people to heavenly life, a savior who could establish the ideals of Heaven, and a savior who could move all people into a position where they could enjoy the love of Heaven with the life and ideals of Heaven. No one among humanity could comprehend the life of Jesus, the feelings He brought, or the love He embodied.

For this reason, Jesus lamented, "If I have told you earthly things and you do not believe, how will you believe if I tell you heavenly things?" (John 3:12) He said, "Foxes have holes and birds of the air have nests, but the Son of Man has nowhere to lay His head." (Matthew 8:20) What was the basis of these words? They were not based on any ideology, philosophy, or any familial, emotional, or social foundation. They were spoken from the heart that envisioned a new ideology and the reality of life that could be enjoyed within that new system, looking forward to a time when those realities could sing eternal love with God.

In this light, Jesus had nowhere to lay His head. He was an exceedingly lonely and pitiful person. Why? Because He came with an inner heart and worldview that were diametrically opposed to the world. The places He stayed were in enemy territory, the environment He lived in was hostile, the sovereignty He was under was that of the enemy, and the world where He sought love was also that of the enemy. Therefore, there could be no peace in His movements. Everything He encountered was an enemy.

In the midst of this, Jesus had the responsibility to establish a life-giving foundation of Heaven and to carry out the movement of openness on behalf of Heaven. He was not the cowardly Jesus who bled on the cross to save all humanity, but rather the Jesus who sought to penetrate the hearts and consciences of countless people, inspiring them to follow Him. His focus was there.

The emotional world without the gap between subject and object
Those who look at the universe through scientific logic, formulas, and laws, and who do not possess an inner emotional resonance that secretly connects them beyond that stage have no further development. This is true for literature, art, philosophy, and religion as well.

And this phenomenon occurs only in a state where they are immersed in their field of expertise.

Today, in Buddhism, people pray for blessings while venerating a statue of Buddha, and although there may be a significant external difference between the subject and the object, in the world of the heart, there is no difference. If everything felt there is treated as heaven and believed in, heaven will not forsake that heart and will fulfill it, which is where the term "wish fulfillment" comes from.

God, who has not been able to sing with nature alongside Adam and Eve in the original Garden of Eden
So, in the original Garden of Eden, did God have a time with Adam and Eve to sing about nature and express feelings towards nature? No, He did not. God must have wanted to say, "My son, look at that mountain. I created it in such and such a way, or look at that vegetation. I created it in such and such a way. All of this was created for your happiness." 
However, God could not actually say such words. Why could He not? Because Adam had not yet matured. However, you must understand that there was a deep inner feeling that God wanted to express while looking at Adam. We must understand God's situation, that He could not speak to Adam because Adam was in a state of immaturity. 
If Adam had been in a position where he could do so, God could have taken his hand and said, "Hey, Adam, let’s look at the flowers in that garden that I want to see together. Let’s look at the mountains and rivers that I want to see together." If our ancestors had lived such a life, today’s humanity would not be struggling in this realm of death and suffering. 
Therefore, today you must long for that. You must long for the original Eden. A world filled with God's infinite love, a world where once you start, you can forever resonate with the feelings of love, a world where once you sing, you can be intoxicated by the song for eternity, a world where once you jump, you want to jump forever with God, a world where once you move and take responsibility, you can think and strive that this is a responsibility of eternal value. You must become a person who can long for such a world. It is God's sorrow that He has not found a person with such feelings. God, who governs the earth, must inevitably find and establish such a person. 
In the songs we sing, nature or the mountains and rivers are included because we are trying to elevate our feelings through all of this. Everything is like that. If Adam and Eve could have gone to God with the same feelings that God wanted to have in the original world, how wonderful would that have been? How wonderful would it have been? 
Now you must have such feelings. A person rich in such feelings, a person who has experienced such feelings will be the one who participates as a citizen of the new era, the era of the new ideal paradise. 
Then, dear ones, if you want to resolve the resentment of restoration and step over the sorrows of history to grasp the glorious hand of God, you must understand what kind of person God will grasp. God will want to hold onto a person who can say, "Enjoy all of this on my behalf. Feel all of this on my behalf. Love all of this on my behalf." 
Dear ones! Have you ever longed in your heart while looking at a single flower of nature in a mysterious or gracious atmosphere? Have you ever treated it with the earnestness of meeting an ancestor? Or when you look at the mountains and rivers, have you ever offered praise to heaven without even realizing it due to the stimuli that come to you? If not, I firmly assert that you do not qualify to be the master of all things. No matter how good the Eden that humanity longs for may be, if it is not a place where humans can move heaven through their hearts while looking at all of creation, it is not a place worth longing for. 
Until now, we have prayed only for humanity. I do not do that. We must pray not only for humanity but also for heaven. We must pray for Jesus. Jesus came to this earth and prayed for us through the night, and we must repay that. Next, we must pray for God, who has worked hard until today, and furthermore, we must pray for all people. A person who lives in such feelings can be said to be the closest to God. I have experienced this. 
If you have such feelings while walking on a tired path or resting, heaven will surely be with you. If that happens, you can hold onto the roots of an old zelkova tree and sing the heart of heaven there, and you can lean against a large shaded rock and make it a resting place to sing the emotions of heaven, can’t you? 
The fallen human who must feel both joy and sorrow regarding all things
Today, we, the members of the Unification Church, are in a position where we must lament the fact that God has a favorite among the good creations He personally made, just as there must be a flower that He loves most among flowers. If one does not have such feelings, they will be a failure in the world of the heart. One must be able to say which flower among flowers, which tree among trees, and which grass among grasses they love the most. Only then will the heart of longing for nature arise. 
A person who can embrace life while it is pulsating and can draw nature in with the emotional connections they have is a person of purpose and cannot live carelessly. 
What kind of nature do we see today, and what kind of land do we tread upon? Sadly, it has become a fallen land, a land where we should not only rejoice but also mourn. You must feel this. When you look at all things, you must feel that while they are pleasant, they are still in a realm of lamentation with sad circumstances. Even if there are beautiful scenic spots that you find pleasant, you must become a person who can feel an infinitely sad emotion and connect it to the Father. 
We must become a person who can hold onto a single blade of grass and feel joy while also being able to cry in sorrow. We must become a person who can reflect on joy and hold onto a tree and cry. We must become a person who can look at the mountains and rivers and sigh deeply. This is because we have a heart that longs for Eden. You must understand that the one who is deeply immersed in such feelings is God, and the one who has not yet escaped from such emotional connections is humanity. If one has such feelings, they will be able to look at nature and long for Eden. If we speak of the longed-for Eden, then nature must also be longed for, and the original person who can govern all of creation within it must also be longed for. 
The true person whom God and all things long for
Jesus prayed for his enemies. He prayed for those who nailed his hands and feet and placed a crown of thorns on his head. He prayed for the reckless enemies who pierced his side with a spear. Why did he do that? It is because he knew well that they were created as a result of the Father’s utmost effort and the deep inner circumstances He went through. Do you understand? 
Jesus, who came with the circumstances of heaven, was in a position of opposition from his enemies, but when he touched upon the original feelings of God, he could not help but pray for those who were created with the connection that God had poured all His energy into. 
During his more than thirty years on earth, Jesus maintained a perfect relationship with God through meditation or imagination. Therefore, he was the true original person, the true original person. He was a person whom all creation could long for and a person whom God could long for. 
Today, if a person wants to finish what they are making and does not complete it today, they will go back tomorrow to continue and finish it completely, God is the same. How joyful He must have been to create humans, and if there is someone who has entered into that emotional world and experienced it, they would want to dance for decades. 
If a person is merely a human who appears through the value of such simple laws as believers speak of today, then such a person is not needed. This is because they were created through an absolute principle with infinite elasticity that cannot be measured by laws, and thus their value is great. When looking at such a person, God could feel His entire attribute and sense the emotions flowing through the entire universe. When He looked at this, God was infinitely joyful. 
Adam and Eve, whom God looked at and rejoiced over, Adam and Eve, whom God longed for, and furthermore, Adam and Eve, who were hoped to become the masters of all creation, what happened to them? Due to the fall, longing turned into curses and resentment, happiness and hope turned into lamentation and despair, life turned into death, and love turned into weeping. This is a shocking reality. 
Even though we are in a position where we must lament the fact that we have such unfortunate ancestors, many among us do not know where this unfortunate reality started and how it relates to us today. Heaven will be looking for those who can break free from this and sweep away the unfortunate feelings, find the original feelings of humanity, rejoice, and raise the voice of that joy. Is there no one who has entered such a place? Heaven will seek them out. 
In this matter of the heart, since a valuable person who can be longed for by heaven and all things has become like this today, they must be judged. I think so. Father! If I wish to escape judgment, I hope to become a person who passes the test of longing for You. I hope to become a victorious person who can sing by passing the heart of wanting to see and meet the heart that rejoiced in placing Adam and Eve in Eden. 
This is what we must pray for. Heaven desires this. 
I must become a person who can long for the heavenly principles while also becoming a person who can long for humanity. God desires to make His heart felt through you.
You should think about how grateful it is to have given birth to a son and a daughter.  
If there are men and women on the earth, they are beings established to represent God's overall character and nature. Therefore, a man should be one who knows how to love a woman, and a woman should be one who knows how to love a man. As beings who possess the heart that Adam desired through God's heart and the heart that Eve desired, if there are couples on the earth who can embrace heaven while enjoying freedom, it is the will of heaven to give them the entire universe and let them rest, which humanity today does not know.  
Because humanity has violated the laws of such a heart, today they are struggling with infinite longing in the world of the heart. They try to fill this longing through various hobbies, art, scholarship, or any object of love on earth, but the reality of fallen humanity is that they struggle without being able to fill it. This is the historical sorrow and tragedy.  
If such longing rises in your heart, you should be able to long for the original garden along with all things that long for the original garden, and you should become a person who can lead God's heart through the original heart and long for heaven. If you become such a person, you should know that God cannot help but embrace you, saying, "Oh my son, my daughter."  
The mission of religion to cultivate a person who can govern the universe  
If you wish to elevate your value and approach heaven, you must listen to the Lord's words and experience the value of being a person who can live in the original garden you long for, and you must have a heart that can respond to the longing for heaven and long for heaven. If such a person appears, how pleased would heaven be?  
Longing cannot be fulfilled without love. That love must be God's love, which is not human love but the source of eternal rest and eternal life. For this reason, Christianity, more than any other religion, seeks to fulfill its mission as a religion of love. The purpose of religion is to cultivate such a person who has the authority to govern all principles of the universe while utilizing the laws of the world of the heart in relation to emotional experiences.  
Though they are like stones, God has established a standard of heart that has longed for us humans for 6,000 years and has been guiding us. History has unfolded in countless ways, but God has consistently maintained that longing from the perspective of Alpha and Omega. If humanity differs from God's heart, that person is a loser and a dropout in the historical journey. Heaven is Alpha and Omega, the beginning and the end. This was a precious noun. Furthermore, we must understand that God has a sad heart towards fallen humanity, longing for them.  
Holding onto this insignificant body, God has not forsaken the heart that longs for this fallen humanity, which has wounded the original heart. If there is someone who feels that heaven has been longing with a trace of sorrow for fallen humanity, that person will surely go to heaven. I once prayed like this:  
"Father! I hope to become a person who can hold onto my own hands and cry out of longing." God must be hoping for that. If God can truly hold onto a hand with love, then that person must be one who can hold onto that hand and cry.  
You must become a person who can hold onto the hands of the original Adam, who longed for God without falling. Furthermore, you must become a person who can hold onto Adam and Eve and cry. If you become such a person, you will rise above the history of the fall.  
We have a historical responsibility to long for the original person and to elevate that value before God. Unknowingly, we try to elevate our own value and set our own individuality as an object of longing, and this is human nature. This is because humans have had such ideals from the beginning. However, if you try to elevate your value and make a mistake, you may end up accepting the values of the fallen world, and if you try to set yourself as an object of longing and make a mistake, you may easily become the basis of the fall.  
For this reason, fallen humanity is entirely negative, and everything must be discarded. This is because Adam and Eve fell from a position where they could not possess everything. Adam and Eve did not have such ideals, nor did they possess any issues of the heart. They could not stand in a position of having the authority to govern all things, and that is what the fall is. Did Adam ever stand in a position to govern all things? He did not.  
Thus, due to the historical conditions that require us to long for the original person and seek him, we must understand that humanity must start from crying and abandon everything. Therefore, when we look for a religion that induces crying, we hear Christianity saying, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is near." Jesus appeared on this earth and said, "Repent, for the kingdom of heaven is near," which means to wail. It means to wail for yourself, for your family, for all the people you love, for your nation, and for the entirety of this earth you live on. We must understand that there is a heavenly intention behind this to establish new connections of longing.  
The problems of life can only be resolved through religion  
We must know how to long for all things and for people. Have you ever longed for people? Have you ever experienced a heart that can connect with the pure heart of heaven and infinitely give without forgetting and enjoy? To induce such a heart, heaven has placed the noun of religion, the noun of the Lord, and the slogan of bride and groom, and has been guiding us. We must be able to give everything for Him.  
God is looking forward to the day when He can receive all things offered in connection with the heart and longing. He desires to receive families offered with a heart filled with longing. God is the one who wishes that this nation, this people, and this world be dedicated with a heart filled with longing.  
You must now be able to say before heaven, "Please accept this coin, which is worth only a penny." At that time, that penny can represent the universe. No matter how humble the family is, when you say, "Please accept this family, though it is lacking," that family can receive the inheritance of heaven. Even the poor nation, the Israelites wandering in the wilderness, when they say, "Please accept this nation with a heart longing for heaven," heaven wanted to grant that nation the leading authority of the heavenly kingdom on earth.  
The same goes for nations and the world. Even if there is some idealism or ideology that must be given to humanity today, if it does not make heaven long for it and does not emotionally yearn for heaven, it cannot solve the fundamental problems of life and cannot resolve the fundamental issues of heavenly principles.  
The fall was the inability to have a moment to long for heaven and to long for the original garden, so the mission of restoration is to establish that relationship by placing my own self in that world.  
If there is a person who can comfort the Father's heart with a heart filled with the intention to fulfill such a mission, who can call heaven Father while operating within the realm of the emotional and longing garden, seeking all things or moving among humans, that person cannot be unknown to heaven. If there is someone who has wandered in search of the original garden with such a heart, we must understand that he is a true person who cannot be unknown to God, to all humanity, or to all creation.  
Therefore, the longing Eden, the beings growing there, the humans living there, and the God who visited there should not deal with separate circumstances but should form a joyful nest where heaven above and all things below can harmonize around one person. The person there is someone whom heaven can love, someone whom humans can honor, and someone who is undoubtedly the true owner whom all things can respect.  
If this work does not conclude, the restoration providence, that is, the overall will established by heaven, will not be able to see the glory of victory at the end, and we too will not be able to fulfill our wishes while lamenting the sorrow of the fall. If that does not happen, we must clearly understand that we cannot build a world equipped with a day of victory on this earth.  
<Prayer> We know that we are humans who must travel an endless journey of restoration, still left with regrets. However, when we pass through the heart of the Father who has labored, the sorrowful history that has been turning will relate to us today, and the relationship of struggle today can become a foundation for creating future connections, and we must understand that this emotional connection will allow us to build a garden of infinite hope, infinite happiness, and infinite longing.  
Father, where is the mountain and river that You can boast of while leading Adam around? Where are the blooming flowers that You wanted to boast of with Adam, where are the growing trees, where is the green meadow, and where is the flowing stream?  
Adam, who could stand in a realm where he could communicate such feelings, fell away from the side of the Father, but now we wish to be joyful beings who can enjoy with all creation, with all humanity, and with all heaven, having the Father whom we long for beside us. I earnestly hope and wish for this, my Father.  
The resentment left by the cross cannot establish a connection without longing, and the place of glory left behind cannot form a connection without a heart that yearns for the garden of ideals. We have understood this, so please allow us to be sons and daughters who can face all things in the original garden as original people with a heart of longing, and let us be blessed children who receive the blessings of our Father without forming connections to the fall, and lead us to become true ancestors of humanity.  
Father, I entrust all of this to You today. I earnestly ask and wish that through the words offered, a new joy will sprout on their hearts. In all things, I pray in Your name. Amen.  
          Selected Words of Rev. Sun Myung Moon <Volume 6>
